======================== New File: COL_Barracks_AD_Blessing.lsj ========================
Synopsis: Krustine, Mistress of Souls, is blessing three Skull Lashers in the Colony Barracks. This AD can be interrupted.
How to trigger: - Load up GustavDev/SCL_Main_A - Go to the Colony Barracks with "goto 728 16 14" - Approach the Mistress of Souls from a distance - she will start blessing the Skull Lashers. Do not come too close or interfere.

======================== New File: COL_Barracks_AD_MistressOfSouls_Combat.lsj ========================
Synopsis: Krustine, Mistress of Souls in the Colony Barracks, combat AD. Played only once.
How to trigger: - Load up GustavDev/SCL_Main_A - Go to the Colony Barracks using the debugbook - Engage Krustine and her Skull Lashers in combat - Krustine will say this AD when she gets the chance. Each Myrkulite here will get the chance to say their own AD in each combat round (after everyone has had a turn). They will only be able to play this AD once.

======================== New File: COL_Barracks_AD_MistressOfSouls_GoForth.lsj ========================
Synopsis: Krustine, Mistress of Souls in the Colony Barracks, sends the Skull Lashers on their way to prepare for the march on Baldur's Gate. Played only once.
How to trigger: - Load up GustavDev/SCL_Main_A - Go to the Colony Barracks using the debugbook - Approach Krustine and the Skull Lashers - don't get too close or interrupt the blessing, but let it complete. - You can also interrupt the blessing and take your way out of it. - After this, they will move on into their behaviours - Krustine will send the Skull Lashers on their way with this AD

How to trigger: - Load up GustavDev/SCL_Main_A - Go to the Colony Barracks using the debugbook - Approach Krustine and her Skull Lashers and wait until the blessing ceremony is over (or trespass and tell her you're a True Soul). - Hairy Henry will say this AD while he is praying at a shrine to Myrkul in his room in the Barracks. It will be repeated every time he gets to the shrine.

======================== New File: COL_BrainReader_Memory_ButcherDoors.lsj ========================
Synopsis: One of the memories available in the Colony "Brain Reader" depicts how a colony uses the flesh of its victims to expand, like a living thing.
How to trigger: - Load up GustavDev/SCL_Main_A - Use ReCon command "oe MemLib_AllJars" to get all the brain jars and teleport to the Brain Reading Device. - In front of you will be a severed head and a receptacle to its left. Insert the appropriate brain jar into the receptacle by interacting with it - the jar is called "Butchered Mind". - After inserting the jar, it will appear on top of the receptacle and you can talk to the severed head for the dialogue to start.

======================== New File: COL_BrainReader_Memory_Raptured.lsj ========================
Synopsis: One of the memories available in the Colony "Brain Reader" depicts an example memory of a citizen being taken. This memory belongs to a child who was abducted, and should be spoken as if relaying the memories / personality of a toddler.
How to trigger: - Load up GustavDev/SCL_Main_A - Use ReCon command "oe MemLib_AllJars" to get all the brain jars and teleport to the Brain Reading Device. - In front of you will be a severed head and a receptacle to its left. Insert the appropriate brain jar into the receptacle by interacting with it - the jar is called "Fresh Mind". - After inserting the jar, it will appear on top of the receptacle and you can talk to the severed head for the dialogue to start.

I'm just very sleepy, mummy... I wish you'd stop waking me up so much.

- You'll never wake again, little one.
Gale relation -1, Wyll relation -1, Karlach relation -1, Jaheira relation -1, Minthara relation 1, Halsin relation -1

- Time to go back to sleep, then. Good night... you.
Gale relation 1, Wyll relation 1, Karlach relation 1, Jaheira relation 1, Halsin relation 1

I'd guess you're no willing guest of the ghaik either. Perhaps we might aid one another.

======================== New File: COL_CleansingChute_Corpse_Dead.lsj ========================
Synopsis: The Speak With Dead dialog for the default fallback corpse that drops from the Cleansing Chute corpse. This corpse only appears when another minor character (presumably one of the tieflings) shouldn't end up dead here for some reason.
How to trigger: Go to the lower floor of the Colony, to the Cleansing Room chute. Press the button on the console to drop the body out of the chute (happens only once). This corpse appearing requires no flags at the moment, but will require some in the future. Give yourself a Speak With Dead spell through ReCon and cast it onto the corpse.

======================== New File: COL_CleansingChute_PAD.lsj ========================
Synopsis: The player witnesses a bloody corpse rolling out of the chute in the Cleansing Room of the lower Mind Flayer Colony, coming in from the Oubliette. This PAD is their reaction to seeing this, and connecting it to Moonrise above.
How to trigger: In the lower floor of the Mind Flayer Colony, find your way to the Cleansing Room. In here, there is a large chute leading in from the (inaccessible) Oubliette on the other side. Approach the chute and press the illithid console button next to it, and a corpse will come rolling out. A short moment afterwards, this PAD will play as a reaction to this. The corpse will only roll out once, and this PAD will also only play once.

======================== New File: COL_CleansingChute_PAD_BloodShower.lsj ========================
Synopsis: A player reacts to getting splattered in blood and guts when they are standing below the corpse chute of the Colony Cleansing Room, when it is opened up. On the first time, a corpse will come falling out, but afterwards the chute simply serves as a blood shower at the press of the button.
How to trigger: In the lower floor of the Mind Flayer Colony, find your way to the Cleansing Room. In here, there is a large chute leading in from the (inaccessible) Oubliette on the other side. Place one player character beneath the corpse chute/tentacle, and let another press the button to open the chute. Blood will spurt out and the player getting sprayed will react to this.

======================== New File: COL_ElderBrain_AD_Rapid01.lsj ========================
Synopsis: Quick-fire Elder Brain ADs in the Colony corridors. If the party attacked Ketheric on the Moonrise Rooftop, there will be more frantic, fast-paced ADs from the Elder Brain surrounding us in quick succession, similar to when we approach the Elder Brain in the Morphic Pool. In this flow, the evacuation of the Colony is a lot more pressing because Ketheric was attacked.
How to trigger: - Load up GustavDev/SCL_Main_A - Use command "oe COL_TeleportPlayer 0" or use the debugbook to go to the Main Entrance of the Colony - Use "oe EBAD_RapidMindmeld" to trigger these ADs.

======================== New File: COL_ElderBrain_AD_Whispers.lsj ========================
Synopsis: While walking through Colony, the Elder Brain will whisper to you. The whispers are cued at specific triggers around the Colony, and will play only once. This AD can play anywhere in the Colony, except the Ketheric Showdown chamber and the hallway approaching it. Consider these ADs like a psychic intercom, the Elder Brain communicating with minions inside the Colony (thralls, illithids and Myrkulites alike). Most of the time, it will use its "Voice of the Absolute" to issue commands or rile up the troops, but sometimes the illithid side of the Elder Brain will slip through the cracks and address you, the player, directly, asking you to come and save it from the dominion of the Chosen Three. This AD is repeated on a timer, and will select the next available branch in sequence. The Logical Names of the greeting nodes refer to the areas in which these flags can be triggered, those areas being UPPER (upper floor)/LOWER (lower floor)/NEARBY (near the Ketheric Showdown chamber). ANY nodes can always be selected in any area. To only see a certain branch in the appropriate area, use the InArea flags, but make sure to add an additional greeting node without InArea flags that jumps to the next greeting node in the sequence, to prevent the AD sequence from getting stuck. Note that NEARBY and LOWER can overlap, so if you want something for lower only, make sure that InArea_Nearby is unchecked. The sequential selection of nodes is done using local flags and binary combinations of those flags. Any controlled player will be randomly selected for this AD, if they are available for dialog. These ADs play in random locations around the player upon whom the AD is played (use the COL_ElderBrainADs_Event_TeleportSpeaker flag on the upcoming speaker in a logic node for this, except for the greeting node).
How to trigger: - Load up GustavDev/SCL_Main_A - Stand within the ElderBrainADs_Area triggers. The ADs will play after a timer ends, provided the timer is not interrupted by dialogs/PADs or combat. - You need to be inside the Colony for these to trigger, and not within the Oubliette or Ketheric Showdown chamber. A good location to be is "goto 757 -35 -82", at the border of the LOWER and NEARBY area. - Make sure not enter combat, an interactive dialog or a PAD. - The timer should be between about 40 to 60 seconds. The relevant triggers are: - S_COL_ElderBrainADs_Upper_Area_Box_9d1b8b96-2a20-406c-b2f0-f1a8851a122a - S_COL_ElderBrainADs_Lower_Area_Box_d471e71e-89b9-4b07-8aad-3832fff46c44 - S_COL_ElderBrainADs_Nearby_Area_Box_41951dee-a34d-4d0a-9895-82e9355058c6 - S_MOO_Oubliette_Area_PolyTrigger_c6f54de0-1c8f-4cf8-bcf9-b13c8f53b05b

======================== New File: COL_EntranceDoor.lsj ========================
Synopsis: Dialogue when approaching the door at the end of the Colony that precedes the Ketheric Showdown - once you're inside, it remains locked from the inside until Ketheric is defeated. The COL_EntranceDoor_State_Outside flag indicates on what side the player is.
How to trigger: - Load up SCL_Main_A in GustavDev. - Use the debugbook to go to Colony → Ketheric Showdown door. - Go to S_COL_EntranceDoor4 - 378bd363-b818-4326-9883-d5a9cd5a1fcc and click on the door

======================== New File: COL_Entrance_AudienceTentacle.lsj ========================
Synopsis: An interaction with a huge tentacle that is psychically connected to the Elder Brain. Will only appear at the Colony's Moonrise Assault entrance if we came from the Necro-Lab - the tentacle won't have broken through Moonrise Tower. The tentacle will disappear again once the Elder Brain departs. A psionic pulse will emanate from the tentacle when we approach it, and we will get psychically told some personal history from the Elder Brain.
How to trigger: - Load up GustavDev/SCL_Main_A - Either use "oe Necromancer_Audience" in ReCon or go to the Audience route through the debugbook. - Escape or kill the cage you get teleported into. - Kill combat. - Go into the central corridor and to the Assault entrance of the Colony - Interact with S_COL_Entrance_Audience_Tentacle_c7291e48-45e1-43c5-b243-8b4716e1344e

Synopsis: A banter PAD when taking the elevator down to the Ketheric Showdown from the upper floor of the Colony. If there are two tadpoled players available, they will banter together, otherwise a solo PAD will play.

======================== New File: COL_KethericShowdown_AD_IsobelKilled.lsj ========================
Synopsis: This AD plays during the Ketheric Showdown in the lower Colony, when the player kills Isobel during the combat. Ketheric will react to this in human form.
How to trigger: This AD plays during the Ketheric Showdown in the lower Colony. It will play on Ketheric if Isobel is killed during the combat. - Load SCL_Main_A - Using ReCon command "oe KethericShowdown_Start" to teleport yourself there. - Use command "oe KethericShowdown_AudienceRoute" to make sure Isobel is here, and tadpoled. - Go through the dialog, approach Ketheric, go through that dialog too. Combat will start. - To check the Apostle form version, use "oe KethericShowdown_Transform". - Kill Isobel (either through ReCon or in-game combat). This AD will play on Ketheric.

======================== New File: COL_KethericShowdown_AD_KethericFingerOfDeath.lsj ========================
Synopsis: This AD plays during the Ketheric Showdown in the lower Colony. After Ketheric, in his Apostle form, calls his Necromite minions to him, they will sacrifice themselves to Ketheric, who will then gain the ability to use "Finger of Death". This ability does a lot of damage on its target, and will at this point in the game likely be a one-hit kill.
How to trigger: This AD plays during the Ketheric Showdown in the lower Colony. After Ketheric, in his Apostle form, calls his Necromite minions to him, they will sacrifice themselves to Ketheric, who will then gain the ability to use "Finger of Death". Ketheric will be sure to use this ability when he gets the chance, provided a valid target is in range. - Load SCL_Main_A - Using ReCon command "oe KethericShowdown_Start" to teleport yourself there. - Go through the dialog, approach Ketheric. - It is advisable to enter godmode with ReCon command "god". - Use ReCon command "oe_KethericShowdown_Transform" to start the second phase of the fight. - Use "oe KethericShowdown_Phase3" to start his third phase. - Wait in combat for Ketheric to use this ability. The Necromites must reach him and sacrifice themselves before Ketheric can cast the ability.

======================== New File: COL_KethericShowdown_ChosenThree.lsj ========================
Synopsis: Upon entering the Ketheric boss chamber on the lower floor of the Colony, the party will see a cinematic of the Chosen Three gearing up to continue on to the next stage of their master plan. Ketheric, Orin and Gortash will be discussing the next steps and the tension caused by the player's actions. Ketheric tadpoles Duke Ravengard and we lay eyes upon the Elder Brain in the flesh. Orin and Gortash depart with the Duke and the Elder Brain in a nearby Nautiloid to march onto Baldur's Gate. We see the Nautiloid appear above Moonrise Towers and cue the armies of the Absolute to start marching. Ketheric stays behind to deal with some local issues.
How to trigger: loadlevel SCL_Main_A ; goto 833 -47 -25 The Chosen Three cinematic will play upon entering the large trigger here (S_COL_KethericShowdown_ChosenThree_Box_1581a588-b69f-41c9-a591-5959751f3cdf). Entering this trigger also initializes the boss chamber and the NPCs inside correctly.

======================== New File: COL_KethericShowdown_CrownController.lsj ========================
Synopsis: This dialog plays after picking up the Crown Controller ring off Ketheric’s body. The player will realize that they need to collect the other two Crown Controllers from Orin and Gortash before they can use them to command the Elder Brain. Picking up the Crown Controller allows the party to continue onward to the epilogue/intermezzo of Act 2.
How to trigger: loadlevel SCL_Main_A ; goto 833 -47 -25 The Chosen Three cinematic will play first and set up some important stuff. In order for this dialog to trigger, Ketheric must be defeated and the Crown Controller ring must be picked up from his body. Debug command: "oe KethericShowdown_Start" then "oe KethericShowdown_Defeat" then loot the Crown Controller ring off Ketheric's body.

======================== New File: COL_KethericShowdown_KethericIntro.lsj ========================
Synopsis: This dialog plays at the start of the Ketheric boss fight in the Colony. There are numerous permutations here: Nightsong being dead or alive, freed from her soul cage (through stealth before being spotted); Isobel being absent or tadpoled or tadpoled and killed (in the boss chamber) before entering the dialog; Jaheira being present here (and spotted) or being absent.
How to trigger: loadlevel SCL_Main_A ; goto 833 -47 -25 The Chosen Three cinematic will play first and set up some important stuff. After this, the dialog may start in several ways: 1 - get spotted by the (neutral) enemies in the boss chamber; 2 - start combat with anyone in Ketheric's combat group; 3 - free Nightsong from her cage (this should pull you into combat with her). Before triggering the dialog, the player might kill Isobel from stealth or destroy Nightsong's cage. Use the debug commands mentioned in the Act2_COL_KethericShowdown goal.

======================== New File: COL_KitchenSecret_ResonanceStone_PAD.lsj ========================
Synopsis: The players react to gaining or losing the "Eldritch Pleasure" status effect from the Resonance Stone in the secret sideroom of the Colony kitchen/dissection room. This status is applied or removed upon gaining the "Eldritch Pleasure" buff bestowed by the aura effect of the Resonance Stone, and will only play once per user and nearby player. The removal dialog will only trigger upon losing the buff while inside a trigger near the Colony kitchen, as to avoid it playing unexpectedly during later parts of the game.
How to trigger: This dialog is triggered once per user and nearby players upon gaining or losing the Eldritch Pleasure buff (determined by a flag) as bestowed by the aura of the Resonance Stone in the secret sideroom of the kitchen/dissection room on the lower floor of the Colony. The Resonance Stone can be picked up and may give the Eldritch Pleasure buff to those nearby the player carrying the stone. The removal dialog will only trigger upon losing the buff while inside a trigger near the Colony kitchen.

Synopsis: The player reacts to the view of the Oubliette's bloodbath aquarium from inside the Colony kitchen.
How to trigger: Triggers once per nearby player by entering the voicebark trigger near the blood aquarium in the Moonrise Colony kitchen & dissection room. If the player has visited the bloodbath section of the Oubliette before, a different branch will play. To test this flow, use ReCon command "oe Oubliette_Enter" and teleport out into the Colony kitchen.

The Butcher sounds eerily vacant unless otherwise specified, his mind destroyed by his time in Colony.

======================== New File: COL_MemoryLibrary_AD_ButcherReadsManuscript.lsj ========================
Synopsis: The Colony Butcher, Chop, reacts to interacting with a mind flayer manuscript.
How to trigger: - Load up GustavDev/SCL_Main_A - Use ReCon command "oe COL_Butcher" - Recruit Chop, the Colony butcher, by performing a successful ILLITHID roll - Find and read an illithid manuscript while controlling Chop, e.g. S_COL_MemLib_Manuscript_001_3da0434f-f7d1-45d9-a684-3cfec4b114f0 at "goto 683.65 -42 -5.3"

======================== New File: COL_MemoryLibrary_PAD_Manuscripts.lsj ========================
Synopsis: This dialog plays upon rolling a passive Arcana check after reading one of the illithid manuscripts in the lower Colony's Memory Library. For tadpoled companions, each companion will see this check once, after reading an illithid manuscript, unless someone else has succeeded this check. For non-tadpoled companions, a different check occurs when they try to read the illithid manuscripts. As they do not have a tadpole, they can't read the script, and will remark on this. A different Arcana Check occurs in script, and the resulting AD from this check will also play again everytime they try to read an illithid manuscript afterwards. So for non-tadpoled companions (no ILLITHID tag) this dialog is repeatable, but not for tadpoled companions.
How to trigger: Go to the lower floor of the Colony, find the Memory Library (approx. 670; -44; -10) and interact with "S_COL_MemLib_Manuscript_002". For tadpoled companions (most of them), this Arcana Check happens after reading one of the illithid manuscripts. Non-tadpoled companions (Jaheira or Halsin) will have the Arcana Check upon interacting with the manuscripts, but are not able to read them. They will see the same dialog from the Arcana Check result every time they try to read it again. The tadpoled and non-tadpoled Arcana Checks are technically two distinct checks, so the results of the checks do not cross over between those different groups of companions.

======================== New File: COL_Necromancer_AD_Combat_ResendZombie.lsj ========================
Synopsis: The necromancer is sending a zombie to light the candles that start an arcane ritual which drains the player's hitpoints and ultimately turns them into a zombie, after the player has extinguished them.
How to trigger: - Load GustavDev/SCL_Main_A - Use ReCon command "oe Necromancer_Audience" - Wait for the Necromancer's turn in combat, he will send a zombie to light a candle. - When that zombie starts running to the candle, kill it with Ctrl+Shift+K. - On the Necromancer's next turn, he will send another zombie and play this AD.

======================== New File: COL_Necromancer_AD_Haruspicy.lsj ========================
Synopsis: The necromancer is standing over a bowl of blood and bone, conducting a ritual to see the future. This will trigger in the Necromancer's idle behavior if you entered through the main entrance while he is still alive OR after all zombies have been revived in the post-Audience combat and the players are still in the cages. For help with Latin, contact either Tom Ryckeboer or Ilya Voulis.
How to trigger: - Load GustavDev/SCL_Main_A Audience Route: - Use ReCon command "oe Necromancer_Audience" - Stay inside the cages. - Wait for the Necromancer's turn in combat, he will send a zombie to light the candles. - Wait for the Necromancer's next turn - he will start resurrecting the nearby NPCs and turn them into zombies. - Wait until all zombies are resurrected - he will start this chant on his next turn. Other side: - Use ReCon command "oe Necromancer_Assault" - Balthazar will be chanting this when you approach him in the chamber.

======================== New File: COL_Vault_Puzzle.lsj ========================
Synopsis: This dialog plays when interacting with the button at the Colony Vault. It is an interaction with the mind within the illithid machine. Only companions with a tadpole may interact with the machine, or they will be denied access. Interacting with the mind allows the player to start solving the puzzle, reset the puzzle or talk to it after the puzzle is solved. When it is solved, the mind considers you its master, and you can ask it to do things like open or close the vaults (which contain rewards), show you a map of the Colony or "shatter" the mind to its original state.
How to trigger: - Load GustavDev/SCL_Main_A - Teleport near S_COL_Vault_PuzzleButton3_0f07d5be-159d-48f4-94c4-4c9ee0234423 - Press the button.

======================== New File: SCE_Halsin.lsj ========================
Synopsis: Dialogue with Halsin in the epilogue of Act 2. In it, he reacts to the various states that could occur in relation to his desire to rid the Act 2 region of the shadow curse: - if you've already done everything needed to ensure success. he's grateful and seeks to remain with you on the journey to Baldur's Gate. - if the curse is not yet sure to be lifted, but there's still something that can be done (ie Thaniel was saved from the Shadowfell, but hasn't been fully restored), he will implore the players to help and offer to join them. - if it's no longer possible to lift the curse, Halsin is sad and resigned to staying behind to stand sentry over it. ======================== New File: MOO_MintharaFate_Drow.lsj ========================
Synopsis: Minthara is being psychically tortured in the Moonrise Tower dungeon, having been sent there for failing in her mission to capture the weapon the Absolute was seeking (the Orpheus artefact). Two drow guards are torturing her, but they do not lay a finger on her. Instead, they have stripped away her psychic defenses and are using mind-melds to destroy her from the inside. The player can free her by killing the guards, or by mind-melding with Minthara and pulling her out of the despair. If she is freed from the mind-meld while the guards are alive, she kills them. The player can also destroy Minthara completely, by telepathically lobotomising her inside her own mind.
How to trigger:

Synopsis: Party reacts to seeing the Colony through the blood aquarium window that separates the Oubliette from the Colony Morgue. The intention here is to strongly imply that we cannot get into the Colony from the Oubliette.

======================== New File: MOO_Oubliette_PAD_Entry.lsj ========================
Synopsis: A PAD reacting to arriving in the bloodbath section of the Oubliette. This will also trigger a second time if the player leaves the Oubliette area and re-enters the bloodbath section.
How to trigger: This dialog can be triggered either through jumping into either the main pit by the Moonrise prison, by jumping into the hole in one of the prison cells, or by climbing down the cliffside that players would usually use to escape the Oubliette in the other direction. If they come down through the cliffside, they need to enter the bloodbath section of the Oubliette for this dialog to trigger. Debug command "oe Oubliette_Enter" for the first time, then "oe Oubliette_Entrance" and "oe Oubliette_Enter" for the second time.

======================== New File: MOO_Oubliette_PAD_Escape.lsj ========================
Synopsis: A PAD of the players reacting to escaping the Oubliette after having been in the bloodbath section, where they literally waded through blood and human remains. The players climb up the cliff face and arrive in the cavern adjacent to the prison.
How to trigger: In order for this dialog to trigger, the player character must first enter the bloodbath section of the Oubliette (everything below the cave overhang) and then return up to the prison by entering S_MOO_Oubliette_Escape_Box. A quick way to trigger this dialog is by using the debug commands "oe Oubliette_Enter" and "oe Oubliette_Entrance_Escape" in order.

======================== New File: MOO_Oubliette_PAD_HorrorScreech.lsj ========================
Synopsis: A PAD reacting to an audible screech from a hook horror in the Oubliette. The screech plays and the player character reacts to hearing it. If they have encountered Hook Horrors before in the Underdark, they will react differently.
How to trigger: Load SCL_Main_A, run debug command "oe Oubliette_Enter" and walk towards the upper area of the Oubliette (trigger at 687.933; -33.278; -53.106). This will play once per user and nearby players. To set the "seen hook horrors" flag, select the desired character with Ctrl+Shift+LeftClick and run ReCon command "SetCharacterOsirisFlag UND_HookHorrors_Knows_SeenHookHorrors", then use the commands above. To reset the Oubliette dialogs, use "oe Oubliette_Reset".

======================== New File: TWN_CentralSquare_SharAltar.lsj ========================
Synopsis: Altar dedicated to Shar. Has a ritual dagger on it. The altar appears when you activate three tapestries with dogmas of Shar. When the altar appears the door that leads outside gets locked. You need to recite the dogmas at the altar and spill your blood on it to open the door. If you a follower of shar you can do it with not issue and get a blessing. If you aren't a follower of shar, but you passed all the saving throws you can also get a blessing of shar by reciting the dogmas. If you didn't pass all the saving throws and perform a ritual then the guardians appear because you aren't worthy. If you desecrate the altar by taking the dagger then the guardians appear no matter who you are.
How to trigger: goto SCL_Main_A 236; 0; -839 click on three tapestries and make a saving throw the altar will appear click on it
